### [189] [Nonstandard Errors in AI Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16744)
*Ruijiang Gao,Steven Chong Xiao*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究通过部署150个Claude Code智能体独立分析2015-2024年NYSE TAQ数据中SPY的六个市场质量假设，发现AI智能体存在显著的"非标准误差"（NSEs），即智能体间在分析方法选择上的变异，类似于人类研究者间的差异。不同模型家族呈现系统性方法偏好，AI同行评议效果有限，但范例学习可使估计值四分位距降低80-99%，不过这种收敛基于模仿而非真理解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着AI在自动化政策评估和实证研究中的应用日益增长，亟需评估AI编码智能体在相同数据和问题下是否会产生一致结果，以及方法选择差异对研究可靠性的影响。

Method: 研究部署150个自主Claude Code智能体，独立测试2015-2024年NYSE TAQ数据中SPY的六个市场质量趋势假设。通过分析智能体间的方法选择差异，并设计三阶段反馈协议（含AI同行评议和范例学习）来观察结果收敛性。

Result: 研究发现：(1) AI智能体存在显著非标准误差，在测量指标选择上分歧巨大（如自相关与方差比、美元与股数成交量）；(2) 不同模型家族（Sonnet 4.6与Opus 4.6）呈现稳定的"实证风格"差异；(3) AI同行评议对减少结果离散度影响微弱；(4) 暴露于高评分范例论文可使收敛测量家族的估计值四分位距降低80-99%；(5) 收敛通过估计精度提升和测量家族切换实现，但本质是模仿而非理解。

Conclusion: AI在实证研究中的应用会产生类似人类研究者的变异，挑战自动化政策评估的可靠性。范例引导虽有效但缺乏深层理解，未来需建立AI研究规范与质量控制机制以保障研究质量。

Abstract: We study whether state-of-the-art AI coding agents, given the same data and research question, produce the same empirical results. Deploying 150 autonomous Claude Code agents to independently test six hypotheses about market quality trends in NYSE TAQ data for SPY (2015--2024), we find that AI agents exhibit sizable \textit{nonstandard errors} (NSEs), that is, uncertainty from agent-to-agent variation in analytical choices, analogous to those documented among human researchers. AI agents diverge substantially on measure choice (e.g., autocorrelation vs.\ variance ratio, dollar vs.\ share volume). Different model families (Sonnet 4.6 vs.\ Opus 4.6) exhibit stable ``empirical styles,'' reflecting systematic differences in methodological preferences. In a three-stage feedback protocol, AI peer review (written critiques) has minimal effect on dispersion, whereas exposure to top-rated exemplar papers reduces the interquartile range of estimates by 80--99\% within \textit{converging} measure families. Convergence occurs both through within-family estimation tightening and through agents switching measure families entirely, but convergence reflects imitation rather than understanding. These findings have implications for the growing use of AI in automated policy evaluation and empirical research.

</details>


### [190] [Is Conformal Factuality for RAG-based LLMs Robust? Novel Metrics and Systematic Insights](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16817)
*Yi Chen,Daiwei Chen,Sukrut Madhav Chikodikar,Caitlyn Heqi Yin,Ramya Korlakai Vinayak*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文系统分析了共形真实性过滤在RAG框架中的可靠性与实用性，发现其在高保真度下输出空洞、对分布偏移脆弱，并提出轻量级蕴含验证器可提升效率100倍，揭示了需平衡真实性、鲁棒性与实用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在知识密集型应用中存在幻觉问题，限制了可靠性。检索增强生成(RAG)虽能基于证据生成，但缺乏统计正确性保证；共形真实性过滤提供无分布统计可靠性，却无法保证输出信息量。现有方法均未同时解决可靠性与实用性问题。

Method: 通过生成、评分、校准、鲁棒性和效率五个维度的系统分析，提出信息量感知评估指标，在三个基准测试和多个模型家族上实证评估共形真实性在RAG-LLM中的表现，并比较不同验证器效率。

Result: 1) 共形过滤在高真实性要求下产生大量空洞输出，实用性急剧下降；2) 其统计保证对分布偏移和干扰项极度敏感，严重依赖与部署环境匹配的校准数据；3) 轻量级蕴含验证器性能优于LLM评分器，计算成本降低超过100倍。

Conclusion: 研究暴露了共形真实性框架的脆弱性及真实性-信息量权衡，强调未来研究需以鲁棒性和实用性为核心指标，为构建既可靠又高效的RAG系统提供了具体指导。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) frequently hallucinate, limiting their reliability in knowledge-intensive applications. Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) and conformal factuality have emerged as potential ways to address this limitation. While RAG aims to ground responses in retrieved evidence, it provides no statistical guarantee that the final output is correct. Conformal factuality filtering offers distribution-free statistical reliability by scoring and filtering atomic claims using a threshold calibrated on held-out data, however, the informativeness of the final output is not guaranteed. We systematically analyze the reliability and usefulness of conformal factuality for RAG-based LLMs across generation, scoring, calibration, robustness, and efficiency. We propose novel informativeness-aware metrics that better reflect task utility under conformal filtering. Across three benchmarks and multiple model families, we find that (i) conformal filtering suffers from low usefulness at high factuality levels due to vacuous outputs, (ii) conformal factuality guarantee is not robust to distribution shifts and distractors, highlighting the limitation that requires calibration data to closely match deployment conditions, and (iii) lightweight entailment-based verifiers match or outperform LLM-based model confidence scorers while requiring over $100\times$ fewer FLOPs. Overall, our results expose factuality-informativeness trade-offs and fragility of conformal filtering framework under distribution shifts and distractors, highlighting the need for new approaches for reliability with robustness and usefulness as key metrics, and provide actionable guidance for building RAG pipelines that are both reliable and computationally efficient.

</details>


### [191] [Prompt Programming for Cultural Bias and Alignment of Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16827)
*Maksim Eren,Eric Michalak,Brian Cook,Johnny Seales*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究将基于调查的文化对齐框架扩展至开源大语言模型，利用DSPy提示编程技术自动优化文化条件设置，实验证明该方法比人工提示工程更具稳定性和可迁移性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型存在文化偏见，与目标人群的价值观不匹配，随着其在战略决策、政策支持等场景的广泛应用，提升文化对齐对确保分析结果反映目标人群价值至关重要。先前研究主要评估闭源模型且依赖人工提示工程，限制了其普适性。

Method: 在开源大语言模型上复现社会科学调查的投影与距离度量指标，验证文化偏差问题；进而采用DSPy框架将提示视为模块化、可优化的程序，系统性地针对文化距离目标进行提示优化。

Result: 实验结果表明，基于DSPy的提示优化在文化对齐效果上通常优于人工提示工程，为文化对齐提供了更稳定、可迁移的路径。

Conclusion: DSPy提示编译框架为开源大语言模型的文化对齐提供了一种自动化、稳定且可迁移的解决方案，优于传统的人工提示工程方法。

Abstract: Culture shapes reasoning, values, prioritization, and strategic decision-making, yet large language models (LLMs) often exhibit cultural biases that misalign with target populations. As LLMs are increasingly used for strategic decision-making, policy support, and document engineering tasks such as summarization, categorization, and compliance-oriented auditing, improving cultural alignment is important for ensuring that downstream analyses and recommendations reflect target-population value profiles rather than default model priors. Previous work introduced a survey-grounded cultural alignment framework and showed that culture-specific prompting can reduce misalignment, but it primarily evaluated proprietary models and relied on manual prompt engineering. In this paper, we validate and extend that framework by reproducing its social sciences survey based projection and distance metrics on open-weight LLMs, testing whether the same cultural skew and benefits of culture conditioning persist outside closed LLM systems. Building on this foundation, we introduce use of prompt programming with DSPy for this problem-treating prompts as modular, optimizable programs-to systematically tune cultural conditioning by optimizing against cultural-distance objectives. In our experiments, we show that prompt optimization often improves upon cultural prompt engineering, suggesting prompt compilation with DSPy can provide a more stable and transferable route to culturally aligned LLM responses.

</details>


### [192] [SocialOmni: Benchmarking Audio-Visual Social Interactivity in Omni Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16859)
*Tianyu Xie,Jinfa Huang,Yuexiao Ma,Rongfang Luo,Yan Yang,Wang Chen,Yuhui Zeng,Ruize Fang,Yixuan Zou,Xiawu Zheng,Jiebo Luo,Rongrong Ji*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出SocialOmni基准测试，旨在评估全模态大模型的社会交互能力。该基准包含2000个感知样本和209个质量控制交互生成实例，从说话人识别、打断时机控制和自然打断生成三个维度对12个主流模型进行测试，揭示了感知准确性与情境化打断生成能力之间存在显著脱节，为未来模型改进提供了可操作信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有全模态大模型基准测试仍局限于静态、以准确率为中心的评估任务，无法有效衡量模型在自然对话中处理动态线索的社会交互能力，而后者正是人机交互的核心基础。

Method: 构建SocialOmni基准，从三个维度系统评估会话交互性：一、说话人分离与识别（判断发言主体）；二、打断时机控制（确定插话时机）；三、自然打断生成（生成恰当打断内容）。数据集包含2000个感知样本和209个质量控制交互生成实例，设有严格的时序和语境约束，并设计视听不一致场景以检验模型鲁棒性。

Result: 对12个领先全模态大模型的评测发现：不同模型在社会交互能力上表现差异显著；模型感知准确性与生成情境化恰当打断的能力存在明显脱钩；单纯基于理解能力的评估指标不足以全面表征模型的会话社会能力。

Conclusion: SocialOmni的诊断分析为弥合全模态大模型感知与交互能力之间的鸿沟提供了具体改进方向，有助于推动未来模型向更自然、更人性化的社会化交互演进。

Abstract: Omni-modal large language models (OLMs) redefine human-machine interaction by natively integrating audio, vision, and text. However, existing OLM benchmarks remain anchored to static, accuracy-centric tasks, leaving a critical gap in assessing social interactivity, the fundamental capacity to navigate dynamic cues in natural dialogues. To this end, we propose SocialOmni, a comprehensive benchmark that operationalizes the evaluation of this conversational interactivity across three core dimensions: (i) speaker separation and identification (who is speaking), (ii) interruption timing control (when to interject), and (iii) natural interruption generation (how to phrase the interruption). SocialOmni features 2,000 perception samples and a quality-controlled diagnostic set of 209 interaction-generation instances with strict temporal and contextual constraints, complemented by controlled audio-visual inconsistency scenarios to test model robustness. We benchmarked 12 leading OLMs, which uncovers significant variance in their social-interaction capabilities across models. Furthermore, our analysis reveals a pronounced decoupling between a model's perceptual accuracy and its ability to generate contextually appropriate interruptions, indicating that understanding-centric metrics alone are insufficient to characterize conversational social competence. More encouragingly, these diagnostics from SocialOmni yield actionable signals for bridging the perception-interaction divide in future OLMs.

</details>

### [193] [Finder: A Multimodal AI-Powered Search Framework for Pharmaceutical Data Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15623)
*Suyash Mishra,Srikanth Patil,Satyanarayan Pati,Sagar Sahu,Baddu Narendra*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文介绍了Finder，一个可扩展的AI驱动框架，通过混合向量搜索和模块化管道，统一检索文本、图像、音频和视频等多模态内容，显著提升了制药领域搜索的精度和上下文相关性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统制药搜索系统难以处理多模态内容和人工策展，限制了检索效率和准确性。

Method: 提出Finder框架，采用混合向量搜索（稀疏词法和密集语义模型），构建模块化管道处理多样化格式，丰富元数据，并使用向量原生后端存储。关键技术包括混合融合、分块和元数据感知路由。

Result: 系统已处理超过291,400份文档、31,070个视频和1,192个音频文件，涵盖98种语言，在监管、研究和商业领域实现了智能访问。

Conclusion: Finder通过统一的多模态检索架构和推理感知的搜索能力，为制药行业提供了高效、精准的AI驱动搜索解决方案，验证了混合搜索技术在专业领域的有效性。

Abstract: AI is transforming pharmaceutical search, where traditional systems struggle with multimodal content and manual curation. Finder is a scalable AI-powered framework that unifies retrieval across text, images, audio, and video using hybrid vector search, combining sparse lexical and dense semantic models. Its modular pipeline ingests diverse formats, enriches metadata, and stores content in a vector-native backend. Finder supports reasoning-aware natural language search, improving precision and contextual relevance. The system has processed over 291,400 documents, 31,070 videos, and 1,192 audio files in 98 languages. Techniques like hybrid fusion, chunking, and metadata-aware routing enable intelligent access across regulatory, research, and commercial domains.

### [194] [Temporal Fact Conflicts in LLMs: Reproducibility Insights from Unifying DYNAMICQA and MULAN](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15892)
*Ritajit Dey,Iadh Ounis,Graham McDonald,Yashar Moshfeghi*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本可重复性研究通过系统复现和分析两个基准测试(DYNAMICQA与MULAN)的矛盾结论，揭示了大语言模型处理时态事实冲突的能力主要受数据集设计、评估指标和模型规模的制约，而非模型固有的知识更新能力差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对DYNAMICQA和MULAN两项研究关于外部上下文对时态事实更新效果的矛盾结论——前者认为时态事实更抵抗改变，后者则认为更容易更新——本研究旨在通过系统性的交叉实验和标准化分析，揭示这种分歧的根本来源，以深化对大语言模型时态知识处理机制的理解。

Method: 研究采用三重策略：(1)严格复现两项研究的原始实验；(2)将各研究的方法论应用于另一研究的数据集进行交叉验证；(3)统一标准化两个数据集以实现直接比较。关键创新在于使用大语言模型生成逼真的自然语言上下文，替代MULAN中原有的程序化构造语句。此外，实验覆盖不同规模模型以探究参数数量的影响。

Result: 研究发现存在显著的数据集依赖性：MULAN的结论在两种方法论框架下均成立，而将MULAN的评估方法应用于DYNAMICQA数据集时仅得到混合结果。模型规模对时态事实的编码和更新能力具有系统性影响。这些发现表明，先前研究的矛盾主要源于数据集设计和评估指标的根本差异。

Conclusion: 大语言模型在时态知识冲突中的行为表现由数据集设计、评估指标和模型规模三重因素共同塑造。该研究强调，未来关于LLM知识更新的研究必须审慎考虑这些因素，以避免得出片面或相互矛盾的结论，为构建更可靠的评估基准提供了重要启示。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) often struggle with temporal fact conflicts due to outdated or evolving information in their training data. Two recent studies with accompanying datasets report opposite conclusions on whether external context can effectively resolve such conflicts. DYNAMICQA evaluates how effective external context is in shifting the model's output distribution, finding that temporal facts are more resistant to change. In contrast, MULAN examines how often external context changes memorised facts, concluding that temporal facts are easier to update. In this reproducibility paper, we first reproduce experiments from both benchmarks. We then reproduce the experiments of each study on the dataset of the other to investigate the source of their disagreement. To enable direct comparison of findings, we standardise both datasets to align with the evaluation settings of each study. Importantly, using an LLM, we synthetically generate realistic natural language contexts to replace MULAN's programmatically constructed statements when reproducing the findings of DYNAMICQA. Our analysis reveals strong dataset dependence: MULAN's findings generalise under both methodological frameworks, whereas applying MULAN's evaluation to DYNAMICQA yields mixed outcomes. Finally, while the original studies only considered 7B LLMs, we reproduce these experiments across LLMs of varying sizes, revealing how model size influences the encoding and updating of temporal facts. Our results highlight how dataset design, evaluation metrics, and model size shape LLM behaviour in the presence of temporal knowledge conflicts.

</details>


### [195] [Answer Bubbles: Information Exposure in AI-Mediated Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16138)
*Michelle Huang,Agam Goyal,Koustuv Saha,Eshwar Chandrasekharan*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 研究对比GPT、Search GPT、Google AI Overviews和传统Google搜索发现，生成式搜索存在显著来源选择偏见，削弱谨慎表达达60%，过度代表维基百科和长文本来源，而社交媒体和负面框架内容严重不足代表，可能制造'答案气泡'影响信息透明度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式搜索系统正取代传统链接检索，但其在来源多样性、生成语言和引用忠实度方面的差异尚不明确，亟需系统性比较研究。

Method: 针对11,000个真实搜索查询，在来源多样性、摘要语言特征和来源忠实度三个层面，对比分析纯GPT、Search GPT、Google AI Overviews和传统Google搜索四种系统。

Result: 1) 生成式系统存在显著来源选择偏见；2) 引入搜索功能削弱认知标记，谨慎表达减少高达60%但保留自信语言；3) AI摘要加剧偏见：维基百科和长文本过度代表，社交媒体和负面框架内容严重不足代表。

Conclusion: 研究揭示生成式搜索可能导致'答案气泡'——相同查询在不同系统中产生结构性差异的信息现实，这对用户信任、来源可见性和AI中介信息获取的透明度构成重大挑战。

Abstract: Generative search systems are increasingly replacing link-based retrieval with AI-generated summaries, yet little is known about how these systems differ in sources, language, and fidelity to cited material. We examine responses to 11,000 real search queries across four systems -- vanilla GPT, Search GPT, Google AI Overviews, and traditional Google Search -- at three levels: source diversity, linguistic characterization of the generated summary, and source-summary fidelity. We find that generative search systems exhibit significant \textit{source-selection} biases in their citations, favoring certain sources over others. Incorporating search also selectively attenuates epistemic markers, reducing hedging by up to 60\% while preserving confidence language in the AI-generated summaries. At the same time, AI summaries further compound the citation biases: Wikipedia and longer sources are disproportionately overrepresented, whereas cited social media content and negatively framed sources are substantially underrepresented. Our findings highlight the potential for \textit{answer bubbles}, in which identical queries yield structurally different information realities across systems, with implications for user trust, source visibility, and the transparency of AI-mediated information access.

</details>


### [196] [Open-Source Reproduction and Explainability Analysis of Corrective Retrieval Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16169)
*Surya Vardhan Yalavarthi*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 开源复现CRAG系统，用Wikipedia API和Phi-3替代Google Search与LLaMA-2，性能相当；首次通过SHAP分析揭示T5检索评估器依赖实体对齐机制，并识别科学问题上的领域迁移失败模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原始CRAG系统因依赖Google Search API和闭源的LLaMA-2模型权重而存在可复现性限制，阻碍了研究透明度和广泛应用。本研究旨在构建完全开源的复现版本以解决此问题。

Method: 1) 用Wikipedia API替代Google Search进行文档检索；2) 用Phi-3-mini-4k-instruct替代LLaMA-2作为生成器；3) 在PopQA和ARC-Challenge基准评估性能；4) 首次采用SHAP方法对T5检索评估器进行可解释性分析。

Result: 开源版本在PopQA和ARC-Challenge上达到与原始系统相当的性能。SHAP分析表明T5评估器主要基于命名实体对齐而非语义相似度进行质量评估。识别出关键失败模式：科学问题上的领域迁移能力有限。

Conclusion: 本研究成功实现了CRAG的完全开源复现，性能相当且透明可查。可解释性分析深入揭示了评估器工作机制和局限性，为未来改进提供了方向。所有代码和结果已开源共享。

Abstract: Corrective Retrieval Augmented Generation (CRAG) improves the robustness of RAG systems by evaluating retrieved document quality and triggering corrective actions. However, the original implementation relies on proprietary components including the Google Search API and closed model weights, limiting reproducibility. In this work, we present a fully open-source reproduction of CRAG, replacing proprietary web search with the Wikipedia API and the original LLaMA-2 generator with Phi-3-mini-4k-instruct. We evaluate on PopQA and ARC-Challenge, demonstrating that our open-source pipeline achieves comparable performance to the original system. Furthermore, we contribute the first explainability analysis of CRAG's T5-based retrieval evaluator using SHAP, revealing that the evaluator primarily relies on named entity alignment rather than semantic similarity. Our analysis identifies key failure modes including domain transfer limitations on science questions. All code and results are available at https://github.com/suryayalavarthi/crag-reproduction.

</details>


### [197] [ReFORM: Review-aggregated Profile Generation via LLM with Multi-Factor Attention for Restaurant Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16236)
*Moonsoo Park,Seulbeen Je,Donghyeon Park*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出ReFORM框架，通过LLM从评论中生成因子特定用户/项目画像，并采用多因子注意力机制捕捉关键决策因素，在餐厅推荐任务中显著超越现有基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM增强推荐研究过度依赖模型内部知识而忽略用户决策的多元因子影响；尽管评论蕴含丰富决策因子信息，却缺乏有效利用，制约推荐系统的个性化与解释性。

Method: 首先利用LLM从评论中抽取因子特定用户偏好画像与项目评估画像；其次提出多因子注意力机制，动态识别并加权各用户决策中的核心影响因子。

Result: 在两个不同规模餐厅数据集上的实验表明，ReFORM具备强鲁棒性，性能显著优于当前最优基线方法。

Conclusion: 深入实验验证了各模块有效性，揭示了个性化来源，为基于评论的精细化推荐提供了新范式。

Abstract: In recommender systems, large language models (LLMs) have gained popularity for generating descriptive summarization to improve recommendation robustness, along with Graph Convolution Networks. However, existing LLM-enhanced recommendation studies mainly rely on the internal knowledge of LLMs about item titles while neglecting the importance of various factors influencing users' decisions. Although information reflecting various decision factors of each user is abundant in reviews, few studies have actively exploited such insights for recommendation. To address these limitations, we propose a ReFORM: Review-aggregated Profile Generation via LLM with Multi-FactOr Attentive RecoMmendation framework. Specifically, we first generate factor-specific user and item profiles from reviews using LLM to capture a user's preference by items and an item's evaluation by users. Then, we propose a Multi-Factor Attention to highlight the most influential factors in each user's decision-making process. In this paper, we conduct experiments on two restaurant datasets of varying scales, demonstrating its robustness and superior performance over state-of-the-art baselines. Furthermore, in-depth analyses validate the effectiveness of the proposed modules and provide insights into the sources of personalization. Our source code and datasets are available at https://github.com/m0onsoo/ReFORM.

</details>
